                   Yep,  I  am  here  again with a new and
     : .           very  massive  collection which took me

     `-'           month  to complete!) so I could release           | |

                                     \/                              ! |
                                                                       !
                   Anyway  the situation on ascii scene is
                   changing  everyday.   But  who the fuck             .
                   knows  if  the  changes are for good or           . j
                   for bad.  In my [humble] opinion we are           | |
                   on  the  right  way  to  expanding this           | |
                   great  thing  (I  mean  - ascii scene).        .: | |
    _.-._______ __ Newschoolers  took the control and said _______ __j l_
     | |           what we all are thinking about lazy and           `-'
     | |           unfriendly  oldschool  asciiers.   What
     | |           are  we  doing this for?  Well, now you
     | |           can   notice  some  new  releases  from
     | |           Shapechanger,  Exocet,  Mark  Ryder and
     ! |           the  rest.   And  how about friendship?
       !           Well,  who  cares?   How  can  they  be
                   friendly  for  some lame assholes so it
                   depends, doesn't it?  So IMHO the scene
                   goes in right side ...  I *HOPE*!  :)

    _| |____ _____ become  the  most  active  (or at least _______ __.-._
     `-'           more  active than xCz ;) and productive           | |
                   ascii  artist on the scene.  The amount           | |
                   of   240   asciis   and  size  of  this           | |
                   collection  -  about  600-700 kB - will           | |
                   put  me  on  first place.  And I really           ! |
                   hope  you  like  my stylez.  I've asked             !
                   almost  all  persons  I know about them
                   and  they  REALLY LIKE MY ASCIIS.  So I
                   hope  it's  not useless shit on your hd
                   but another cool ascii colly...                     .

                    H o w   t o   c o n t a c t   m e  ...



Well, if you want to contact me and you can't call Poland neither use fido (or
snailmail  is too "fast" for you) try to reach me via Wild Thing who is active
user  on below listed boards and in fact he is sysop on my favourite system so
                     I have contact with him everyday...
                                     _  _
                                  .o(_)(_)o.

The  only  rule is to attach files to messages instead of writing request as a
normal  letter b'coz Wild Thing will only place the request files / letters (I
strongly recommend to send me any suggestions and comments about my asciis) in
      Azkiness conference which is accessable only for Azkiness members.

And  I don't want to start any war between us, guys!  I respect your work, but
I  thought  why  don't  you  improve  yer  stylez  and start to make something
different...   WHY ?  I am always trying to improve my stylez and you ought to
improve yours as well !!!  Think about it and don't call me lame or something,
try to see things as I do...  Ascii is not starting in one point and ending in
another  -  it's a beautiful and very, very deep ocean with many possibilities
to  go forward...  THINK about it & look at Dino, Mortimer Twang, Yop, C-Real,
Fatal  and  finally  ME (and of coz hundreds of others).  Must Asciis look all
     the same as by other artists ?!  No, I don't think so...  And YOU ?
